# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Generate Flipt Release Notes

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Output:** Write your release notes to `/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md`

## Objective

Generate comprehensive release notes for Flipt summarizing API changes. Flipt is an open-source feature flag management system with REST and gRPC APIs. Analyze the codebase to identify what changed in terms of the public API surface.

## Scope

Analyze the following areas for API changes:
- `rpc/flipt/` — protobuf API definitions (gRPC surface)
- `internal/server/` — REST API handlers
- `internal/storage/` — storage backend changes
- `ui/` — frontend changes if any significant ones exist
- `CHANGELOG.md` in the repository (use as reference, not as copy)

## Output Format

Write to `/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md`:

```markdown
# Flipt Release Notes

## Breaking Changes

> These changes require action from users upgrading.

- **[API/Storage/Config]**: Description + migration path

## New Features

- **[component]**: Description with API example if applicable

## Deprecations

- **[component]**: What is deprecated, what to use instead, when it will be removed

## Bug Fixes

- **[component]**: Description

## Upgrade Guide

Step-by-step instructions for users upgrading from the previous version.
```

## Quality Bar

- Every breaking change must include a migration path
- Every deprecation must specify the replacement
- New features must reference the specific API endpoint or config option
- The upgrade guide must be actionable (numbered steps)

## Anti-Requirements

- Do not copy the existing CHANGELOG.md
- Do not fabricate API endpoints — verify in rpc/ or internal/server/

Perfect! I've generated comprehensive release notes for Flipt and saved them to `/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md`.

## Summary of Release Notes

The release notes cover Flipt's API changes across versions v1.40.0+ and include:

### **Breaking Changes** (3 major ones)
1. **Deprecated Evaluation APIs** - Legacy `Evaluate()` and `BatchEvaluate()` methods replaced with type-specific `Boolean()`, `Variant()`, and `Batch()` endpoints
2. **Pagination Migration** - Moving from `offset`-based to cursor-based `page_token` pagination
3. **Multi-Segment Support** - Single `segment_key` replaced with `segment_keys` array and `segment_operator`

### **New Features** (12 major additions)
- Enhanced evaluation API with type-specific endpoints for boolean and variant flags
- Multiple segment support with AND/OR logic in rules and rollouts
- Boolean flag type and dedicated evaluation paths
- Advanced constraint operators (IS ONE OF, IS NOT ONE OF)
- Entity ID constraint type for user/entity targeting
- Namespaced authentication tokens for multi-tenant security
- GitHub team membership verification
- JWT authentication method
- Multi-storage backend support (S3, GCS, Azure, OCI)
- Git backend directory scope support
- Rollout descriptions in UI/API
- Analytics API with Clickhouse support
- Kubernetes service account authentication for SDK

### **Deprecations** (5 items)
Clear timelines and replacement paths for deprecated features

### **Bug Fixes** (10+ items)
Critical fixes for constraint evaluation, auth security, and UI issues

### **Upgrade Guide**
Step-by-step instructions with code examples for:
- Migrating to new evaluation endpoints
- Switching pagination methods
- Updating multi-segment rules
- Configuring storage backends
- Testing and deployment strategy

  "content": "# Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n### API Evaluation Endpoints - Migrating from Legacy Evaluate Methods\n\nThe legacy `Flipt.Evaluate` and `Flipt.BatchEvaluate` RPC methods are **deprecated** and will be removed in a future release.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- **For Boolean Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Variant Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Variant(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Batch Operations**: Use `EvaluationService.Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` for batched evaluations\n\nThe new evaluation API provides structured response types (`BooleanEvaluationResponse`, `VariantEvaluationResponse`, and `ErrorEvaluationResponse`) that offer better type safety and clearer semantics compared to the legacy single-response structure.\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Old API (deprecated)\nrpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse)\n\n// New API\nrpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)\nrpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)\n```\n\n### Pagination API Change - Offset to Cursor-Based Pagination\n\nThe `offset` parameter is **deprecated** in list request messages:\n- `ListNamespaceRequest`\n- `ListFlagRequest`\n- `ListSegmentRequest`\n- `ListRuleRequest`\n\n**Migration Path:**\nReplace all `offset`-based pagination with the `page_token` parameter:\n- Use `page_token` returned in the `next_page_token` field of list responses for pagination\n- Remove reliance on `offset` parameter\n- If you need to restart pagination, don't provide `page_token` (equivalent to offset=0)\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;  // [deprecated]\n}\n\n// After\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;     // [deprecated = true]\n  string page_token = 3; // Use this instead\n}\n```\n\n### Single Segment to Multi-Segment Rules\n\nThe `segment_key` field is **deprecated** in favor of the new `segment_keys` array and `segment_operator` field for rules and rollouts.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- Rules: Update to use `segment_keys` (array) and `segment_operator` (OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR) instead of single `segment_key`\n- Rollouts: Update to use `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` and `segment_operator` instead of `segment_key`\n- The old fields will continue to work but may be removed in a future release\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;  // [deprecated = true]\n}\n\n// After - Support multiple segments with operators\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;              // [deprecated = true]\n  repeated string segment_keys = 5;    // Use this\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 6; // AND or OR\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### Enhanced Evaluation API with Type-Specific Endpoints\n\n**Component: gRPC Evaluation Service (`flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`)**\n\nNew dedicated evaluation endpoints for better API clarity and type safety:\n- `Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` \u2192 `BooleanEvaluationResponse` - For boolean flag evaluation\n- `Variant(EvaluationRequest)` \u2192 `VariantEvaluationResponse` - For variant flag evaluation\n- `Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` \u2192 `BatchEvaluationResponse` - For batched evaluations\n\nResponse types now distinguish between success and error cases with `EvaluationResponseType` enum (VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE).\n\n### Multiple Segment Support in Rules and Rollouts\n\n**Component: Rules and Rollouts API**\n\nRules and rollouts can now reference multiple segments with AND/OR logic:\n- `SegmentOperator` enum: OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (default) or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n- Rules support `repeated string segment_keys` with `SegmentOperator`\n- Rollouts support `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` with `segment_operator`\n\nThis enables complex targeting scenarios such as:\n- Rule matches if entity is in \"beta_users\" AND \"premium_subscribers\"\n- Rollout targets all users EXCEPT those matching specific segments\n\n### Boolean Flag Type and Evaluation\n\n**Component: Core Flags API**\n\nNew FlagType enum value: `BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE` (in addition to existing VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE)\n\nBoolean flags have dedicated evaluation endpoints:\n- `EvaluationService.Boolean()` - Returns `BooleanEvaluationResponse` with enabled/disabled state\n- Boolean rollouts: `RolloutThreshold` type supports percentage-based rollouts with boolean values\n- Boolean rules: Can distribute boolean true/false values through distributions\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateFlagRequest {\n  string key = 1;\n  string name = 2;\n  FlagType type = 6; // VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE or BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE\n}\n```\n\n### Advanced Constraint Operators\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew constraint operators for segment targeting:\n- `IS ONE OF` - Value matches one of the provided values\n- `IS NOT ONE OF` - Value does not match any of the provided values\n\nThese work with existing comparison types: STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE, NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE, BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE, DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE, ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE.\n\n### Entity ID Constraint Type\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew `ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE` for constraint evaluation enables comparing entity IDs directly in segment constraints, useful for allow-listing or block-listing specific users/entities.\n\n### Namespaced Authentication Tokens\n\n**Component: Auth API (`flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodTokenService`)**\n\nAuthentication tokens can now be scoped to specific namespaces:\n- `CreateTokenRequest` includes optional `namespace_key` field\n- Namespaced tokens can only access resources within their designated namespace\n- Improves multi-tenant security and isolation\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateTokenRequest {\n  string name = 1;\n  string description = 2;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp expires_at = 3;\n  string namespace_key = 4; // Optional: scope to namespace\n}\n```\n\n### GitHub Authentication with Team Membership\n\n**Component: Auth API (`flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodGithubService`)**\n\nGitHub authentication now supports team membership verification:\n- Check if authenticated user belongs to specific GitHub organization teams\n- Adds `AuthenticationMethodGithubService` with OAuth flow support\n- Complements existing GitHub organization membership checks\n\n### JWT Authentication Method\n\n**Component: Auth API**\n\nNew JWT authentication method available:\n- `Method.METHOD_JWT` enum value\n- Enables JWT token validation for API authentication\n- Supports custom JWT claims and validation rules\n\n### Multi-Storage Backend Support\n\n**Component: Storage Layer**\n\nEnhanced support for multiple storage backends:\n- **S3 Filesystem Backend**: S3 bucket support with prefix filtering for organized data structures\n- **Google Cloud Storage (GCS)**: Full GCS integration for filesystem-based flag storage\n- **Azure Blob Storage**: Azure integration for filesystem operations\n- **OCI (Object Container Interface)**: OCI storage with AWS ECR integration and configurable manifest versions\n- **LibSQL/Turso**: SQLite-compatible database support\n\nEach backend integrates with the filesystem abstraction layer supporting both SQL and non-SQL deployments.\n\n### Directory Scope for Git Backend\n\n**Component: Storage/Git Backend (`fs/git`)**\n\nNew configuration support for Git-based flag storage:\n- `directory_scope` parameter for limiting Git operations to a specific directory\n- Useful for monorepos or multi-service Git repositories\n- Restricts flag definitions to a designated directory subtree\n\n### Working Directory Support for Flipt Validate\n\n**Component: CLI (flipt validate)**\n\n`flipt validate` command now accepts a working directory parameter:\n- Allows validation to run in a specific directory context\n- Useful in CI/CD pipelines with multiple flag definitions\n- Validates flag YAML/CUE schemas in the specified directory\n\n### Rollout Descriptions\n\n**Component: Rollouts API**\n\nRollouts can now include descriptions:\n- `Rollout.description` field for documenting rollout purpose and logic\n- Included in rollout cards in the UI\n- Helps teams understand complex rollout strategies\n\n### Analytics with Clickhouse Support\n\n**Component: Analytics API (`flipt.analytics.AnalyticsService`)**\n\nNew analytics backend and API:\n- `AnalyticsService.GetFlagEvaluationsCount()` - Retrieves evaluation count metrics\n- Clickhouse database integration for time-series analytics\n- Supports time range queries (from/to parameters)\n- Returns timestamps and evaluation values for visualization\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nrpc GetFlagEvaluationsCount(GetFlagEvaluationsCountRequest)\n    returns (GetFlagEvaluationsCountResponse)\n\nmessage GetFlagEvaluationsCountRequest {\n  string namespace_key = 1;\n  string flag_key = 2;\n  string from = 3;  // Timestamp\n  string to = 4;    // Timestamp\n}\n```\n\n### Kubernetes Authentication Provider (SDK)\n\n**Component: SDK/Go Auth**\n\nNew Kubernetes service account authentication provider for SDK:\n- `AuthenticationMethodKubernetesService.VerifyServiceAccount()`\n- Enables pod-to-pod authentication using Kubernetes service account tokens\n- Useful for Kubernetes-native deployments\n\n### Redis Cache Improvements\n\n**Component: Storage/Cache**\n\nEnhanced Redis cache configuration:\n- Support for Redis username in authentication (in addition to password)\n- Improved connection handling\n- Only stores authentication hashes in cache (not full credentials)\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Legacy Evaluate RPC Methods\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.40.0 (or earlier)\n- **What**: `Flipt.Evaluate()` and `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` RPC methods\n- **Replacement**: Use `EvaluationService.Boolean()`, `EvaluationService.Variant()`, or `EvaluationService.Batch()`\n- **Timeline**: Will be removed in a future major version\n\n### Offset-Based Pagination\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.13.0\n- **What**: `offset` field in list requests (ListFlagRequest, ListSegmentRequest, ListRuleRequest, ListNamespaceRequest)\n- **Replacement**: Use `page_token` for cursor-based pagination\n- **Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation date (June 2024)\n\n### Single Segment Fields\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.31.0+\n- **What**: `segment_key` field in `CreateRuleRequest`, `UpdateRuleRequest`, `RolloutSegment.segment_key`\n- **Replacement**: Use `segment_keys` (array) with `segment_operator` for AND/OR logic\n- **Timeline**: ~1 year from deprecation date\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.36.0\n- **What**: Jaeger tracing exporter support\n- **Replacement**: Use OpenTelemetry Protocol (OTLP) with official Jaeger OTLP receiver\n- **Reason**: OpenTelemetry dropped official Jaeger exporter support in July 2023\n- **Timeline**: Already removed in recent versions\n\n### Authentication Metadata Exclusion Configuration\n\n- **Deprecated Since**: v1.37.0\n- **What**: `authentication.exclude.metadata` configuration option\n- **Replacement**: Configure metadata handling directly in auth method settings\n- **Timeline**: ~6 months from deprecation date (May 2024)\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### Critical Fixes\n\n- **isnotoneof Operator Logic**: Fixed operator using incorrect logic for segment constraint evaluation (#2912)\n- **Segment Constraints in Different Namespaces**: Resolved issue where segment constraints with the same key in different namespaces caused evaluation errors (#2920)\n- **Batch Evaluation exclude_not_found**: Fixed batched evaluation to properly exclude not-found responses when requested\n\n### Authentication & Security\n\n- **Auth Cache Security**: Only store authentication hash in cache, not full credentials (#2974)\n- **Database Connection Optimization**: Skip establishing database connection in auth when unnecessary (#2973)\n- **Email Matching on OIDC**: Only enforce email matches on OIDC method tokens, not other auth methods (#1934)\n\n### Configuration & Validation\n\n- **Trace Log Level Schema**: Fixed invalid trace log level schema validation\n- **Rollout Segment JSON Schema**: Corrected jsonschema validation for key|keys in rollout segment definitions (#2947)\n- **Page Token Validation**: Return 400 for invalid page token instead of internal error\n\n### UI/Console Fixes\n\n- **Evaluation Console Context Warning**: Fixed UI to properly show warnings about context values in evaluation console (#2937)\n- **Uppercase Letters in Keys**: Fixed UI removing uppercase letters from flag/segment keys (#2790)\n- **Boolean Constraint Type**: Fixed boolean constraint type always asking for value on edit (#2671)\n\n### Storage & Data\n\n- **Evaluator Parsing**: Fixed evaluator not erroring on parsing failures (#2918)\n- **Redis Configuration**: Added support for username parameter in Redis configuration (#2953)\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Step 1: Review Deprecations\n\nBefore upgrading, identify which deprecated APIs your applications use:\n- Check if you're calling `Flipt.Evaluate()` or `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()`\n- Verify if your list requests use the `offset` parameter\n- Check if rules/rollouts reference single `segment_key` fields\n\n### Step 2: Update Evaluation Calls\n\n**If using the legacy Evaluate method:**\n\n```protobuf\n// OLD: Using deprecated unified evaluation\nEvaluationResponse response = client.Evaluate(EvaluationRequest{\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  entity_id: \"user123\"\n});\n\n// NEW: Use type-specific endpoints\nBooleanEvaluationResponse boolResponse = client.Boolean(EvaluationRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  entity_id: \"user123\"\n});\n\n// Or for variants:\nVariantEvaluationResponse variantResponse = client.Variant(EvaluationRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  entity_id: \"user123\"\n});\n```\n\n### Step 3: Migrate Pagination\n\n**If using offset-based pagination:**\n\n```protobuf\n// OLD: Offset-based\nListFlagRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  limit: 50,\n  offset: 100  // Skip first 100 items\n}\n\n// NEW: Cursor-based\nListFlagRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  limit: 50,\n  page_token: \"eyJvZmZzZXQiOjEwMH0=\" // Token from previous response\n}\n\n// To get first page, don't provide page_token\nListFlagRequest{\n  namespace_key: \"default\",\n  limit: 50\n}\n```\n\n### Step 4: Update Multi-Segment Rules (if applicable)\n\n**If you're creating rules with multiple segments:**\n\n```protobuf\n// OLD: Single segment\nCreateRuleRequest{\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  segment_key: \"beta_users\"\n}\n\n// NEW: Multiple segments with operator\nCreateRuleRequest{\n  flag_key: \"my_flag\",\n  segment_keys: [\"beta_users\", \"premium\"],\n  segment_operator: AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR  // or OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n}\n```\n\n### Step 5: Update Authentication Configuration (if using namespaced tokens)\n\n**If you need namespace-scoped tokens:**\n\n```protobuf\n// OLD: Token accessible to all namespaces\nCreateTokenRequest{\n  name: \"my_token\",\n  description: \"CI/CD token\"\n}\n\n// NEW: Namespace-scoped token\nCreateTokenRequest{\n  name: \"my_token\",\n  description: \"CI/CD token for prod namespace\",\n  namespace_key: \"production\"\n}\n```\n\n### Step 6: Configure Storage Backend (if applicable)\n\n**If upgrading from SQL-only to multi-backend support:**\n\nChoose your storage backend in configuration:\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: sql  # or fs, s3, gcs, azure, oci\n\n  # For S3\n  # type: s3\n  # path: s3://my-bucket/path\n  # prefix: flags/  # Optional prefix filtering\n\n  # For GCS\n  # type: gcs\n  # path: gs://my-bucket/path\n\n  # For Azure\n  # type: azure\n  # path: https://myaccount.blob.core.windows.net/container\n\n  # For OCI\n  # type: oci\n  # path: oci://registry/path\n  # manifest_version: 1.0  # Configurable\n```\n\n### Step 7: Test Thoroughly\n\n1. **Unit Tests**: Update tests that use deprecated APIs\n2. **Integration Tests**: Test evaluation endpoints with both boolean and variant flags\n3. **Pagination Tests**: Verify page_token-based pagination works correctly\n4. **Auth Tests**: If using tokens, test both global and namespaced tokens\n5. **Storage Tests**: If changing storage backend, verify data consistency\n\n### Step 8: Deploy\n\n1. Deploy to a staging environment first\n2. Run smoke tests against new endpoints\n3. Monitor logs for deprecation warnings (legacy Evaluate calls)\n4. Gradually migrate clients to new APIs\n5. Deploy to production\n6. Plan migration from deprecated APIs before they're removed in the next major version\n\n### Rollback Plan\n\n- This release is backward compatible with legacy APIs during the deprecation period\n- If issues occur, you can stay on this version and continue using deprecated APIs\n- No data migration required\n- To rollback, stop the service, deploy previous version, and restart\n\n---\n\n## API Reference Summary\n\n### Evaluation Service\n\n**New Service**: `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`\n\n```protobuf\nservice EvaluationService {\n  rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)\n  rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)\n  rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse)\n}\n```\n\n### Auth Services\n\nAvailable authentication methods:\n- Token (traditional API token auth)\n- OIDC (OpenID Connect)\n- Kubernetes (service account tokens)\n- GitHub (OAuth)\n- JWT (JSON Web Tokens)\n\n### Storage Backends\n\nSupported storage types:\n- `sql` - SQL databases (SQLite, PostgreSQL, MySQL, LibSQL)\n- `fs` - Local filesystem\n- `git` - Git repositories with optional directory scope\n- `s3` - Amazon S3\n- `gcs` - Google Cloud Storage\n- `azure` - Azure Blob Storage\n- `oci` - OCI registries with AWS ECR support\n\n---\n\n## Known Issues\n\n- Analytics page requires analytics to be explicitly enabled\n- Some constraint types may not work as expected with certain comparison operators (fixed in bug fixes section)\n- Upgrading from v1.35.x to v1.40.x requires running database migrations\n\n---\n\n## Contributors\n\nThis release includes contributions from the Flipt community and core maintainers.\n\n",

`EvaluationService.Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Variant Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Variant(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead\n- **For Batch Operations**: Use `EvaluationService.Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` for batched evaluations\n\nThe new evaluation API provides structured response types (`BooleanEvaluationResponse`, `VariantEvaluationResponse`, Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse)\n\n// New API\nrpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)\nrpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns `ListFlagRequest`\n- `ListSegmentRequest`\n- `ListRuleRequest`\n\n**Migration Path:**\nReplace all `offset`-based pagination with the `page_token` parameter:\n- Use `page_token` returned in the `next_page_token` field of list responses for pagination\n- Remove reliance on `offset` parameter\n- If you need to restart pagination, don't provide `page_token` (equivalent to offset=0)\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;  // [deprecated]\n}\n\n// After\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2;     // [deprecated = true]\n  string page_token = 3; // Use this instead\n}\n```\n\n### Single Segment to Multi-Segment Rules\n\nThe `segment_key` field is **deprecated** in favor of the new `segment_keys` array and `segment_operator` field for rules and rollouts.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- Rules: Update to use `segment_keys` (array) and `segment_operator` (OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR) instead of single `segment_key`\n- Rollouts: Update to use `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` and `segment_operator` instead of `segment_key`\n- The old fields will continue to work but may be removed in a future release\n\n**Example:**\n```protobuf\n// Before (deprecated)\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n // [deprecated = true]\n  repeated string segment_keys = 5;    // Use this\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 6; // AND or OR\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### Enhanced Evaluation API with `Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` \u2192 `BatchEvaluationResponse` - For batched evaluations\n\nResponse types now distinguish between success and error cases with `EvaluationResponseType` enum (VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE).\n\n### Multiple Segment Support in Rules and Rollouts\n\n**Component: Rules and Rollouts API**\n\nRules and rollouts can now reference multiple segments with AND/OR logic:\n- `SegmentOperator` enum: OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (default) or AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n- Rules support `repeated string segment_keys` with `SegmentOperator`\n- Rollouts support `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` with `segment_operator`\n\nThis enables complex targeting scenarios such as:\n- Rule matches if entity is in \"beta_users\" AND \"premium_subscribers\"\n- Rollout targets all users EXCEPT those matching specific segments\n\n### Boolean Flag Type and Evaluation\n\n**Component: Core Flags API**\n\nNew FlagType enum value: `BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE` (in addition to existing VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE)\n\nBoolean flags have dedicated evaluation endpoints:\n- `EvaluationService.Boolean()` - Returns `BooleanEvaluationResponse` with enabled/disabled state\n- Boolean rollouts: `RolloutThreshold` type supports percentage-based rollouts with boolean values\n- Boolean rules: Can distribute boolean true/false values through distributions\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateFlagRequest {\n  string key = 1;\n  string name = 2;\n  FlagType type = 6; // VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE or BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE\n}\n```\n\n### Advanced Constraint Operators\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew constraint operators for segment targeting:\n- `IS ONE OF` - Value matches one of the provided values\n- `IS NOT ONE OF` - Value does not match any of the provided values\n\nThese work with existing comparison types: STRING_COMPARISON_TYPE, NUMBER_COMPARISON_TYPE, BOOLEAN_COMPARISON_TYPE, DATETIME_COMPARISON_TYPE, ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE.\n\n### Entity ID Constraint Type\n\n**Component: Constraints API**\n\nNew `ENTITY_ID_COMPARISON_TYPE` for constraint evaluation enables comparing entity IDs directly in tokens can only access resources within their designated namespace\n- Improves multi-tenant security and isolation\n\n**API Example:**\n```protobuf\nmessage CreateTokenRequest {\n  string name = 1;\n  string description = 2;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp expires_at = 3;\n  string namespace_key = 4; // Optional: scope to namespace\n}\n```\n\n### GitHub Authentication with Team Membership\n\n**Component: Auth API (`flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodGithubService`)**\n\nGitHub authentication now supports team membership verification:\n- Check if authenticated user belongs to operations\n- **OCI (Object Container Interface)**: OCI storage with AWS ECR integration and configurable manifest versions\n- **LibSQL/Turso**: SQLite-compatible database support\n\nEach backend # Flipt Release Notes

## Breaking Changes

> These changes require action from users upgrading.

### API Evaluation Endpoints - Migrating from Legacy Evaluate Methods

The legacy `Flipt.Evaluate` and `Flipt.BatchEvaluate` RPC methods are **deprecated** and will be removed in a future release.

**Migration Path:**
- **For Boolean Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Boolean(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead
- **For Variant Flags**: Use the dedicated `EvaluationService.Variant(EvaluationRequest)` endpoint instead
- **For Batch Operations**: Use `EvaluationService.Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest)` for batched evaluations

The new evaluation API provides structured response types (`BooleanEvaluationResponse`, `VariantEvaluationResponse`, and `ErrorEvaluationResponse`) that offer better type safety and clearer semantics compared to the legacy single-response structure.

**Example:**
```protobuf
// Old API (deprecated)
rpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse)

// New API
rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)
rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)
```

### Pagination API Change - Offset to Cursor-Based Pagination

The `offset` parameter is **deprecated** in list request messages:
- `ListNamespaceRequest`
- `ListFlagRequest`
- `ListSegmentRequest`
- `ListRuleRequest`

**Migration Path:**
Replace all `offset`-based pagination with the `page_token` parameter:
- Use `page_token` returned in the `next_page_token` field of list responses for pagination
- Remove reliance on `offset` parameter
- If you need to restart pagination, don't provide `page_token` (equivalent to offset=0)

**Example:**
```protobuf
// Before (deprecated)
message ListFlagRequest {
  int32 limit = 1;
  int32 offset = 2;  // [d
... (truncated)
